      const title = document.createElement("p");
      title.className = "djep-events-section-title";
      title.textContent = sectionTitle;
      section.append(title);
    }

    const sectionBody = document.createElement("div");
    sectionBody.className = "djep-events-section-body";

    const eventCards = Array.from(eventListBox.querySelectorAll(".djep-singleeventdiv"));
    if (eventCards.length) {
      eventCards.forEach((card) => {
        const nextCard = document.createElement("div");
        nextCard.className = "djep-events-event-card";
        const eventData = extractEventCardData(card);
        const shell = buildEventsEventShell(eventData);
        replaceEventCardContents(nextCard, eventData.hiddenInfo, shell);
        sectionBody.append(nextCard);
      });
    } else {
      const bodyText = cleanText(
        Array.from(eventListBox.childNodes)
          .filter((node) => node !== titlebar)
          .map((node) => node.textContent || "")
          .join(" ")
      );

      const emptyState = document.createElement("div");
      emptyState.className = "djep-events-empty-state";
      emptyState.textContent =
        bodyText && bodyText.toLowerCase() !== "none found"
          ? bodyText
          : sectionTitle.toLowerCase().includes("past")
            ? "No past events found."
            : "No upcoming events found.";
      sectionBody.append(emptyState);
    }

    section.append(sectionBody);
    return section;
  }

  function mountEventsWorkspace(content, { heading, sections }) {
    if (!(content instanceof HTMLElement)) return;

    const root = document.createElement("div");
    root.id = "page_eventslist";
    root.className = "djep-eventslist-root";

    if (heading instanceof HTMLElement) {
      root.append(heading);
    }

    sections.forEach((section) => {
      if (section instanceof HTMLElement) {
        root.append(section);
      }
    });

    content.replaceChildren(root);
    content.classList.add("djep-events-content");
  }

  function replaceEventCardContents(card, hiddenInfo, shell) {
    Array.from(card.children).forEach((child) => child.remove());
    if (hiddenInfo) {
      card.append(hiddenInfo);
    }
    card.append(shell);
  }

  function addPanelNotes(panels, noteClassName, panelNotes) {
    panels.forEach((panel) => {
      const titlebar = panel.querySelector(":scope > .djep-titlebarsmall");
      if (!titlebar || titlebar.nextElementSibling?.classList?.contains(noteClassName)) return;

      const noteText = panelNotes.get(cleanText(titlebar.textContent));
      if (!noteText) return;

      const note = document.createElement("p");
      note.className = noteClassName;
      note.textContent = noteText;
      titlebar.insertAdjacentElement("afterend", note);
    });
  }

  function cleanupWorkspaceColumns(columns, selectors) {
    columns.forEach((column) => {
      column?.querySelectorAll(selectors).forEach((node) => node.remove());
    });
  }

  function normalizePlanPageHeading(heading, { eventDate, eventDateText, focusTitle, longEventDate }) {
    if (!(heading instanceof HTMLElement) || heading.dataset.djepPlanHeadingInit) return;
    heading.dataset.djepPlanHeadingInit = "1";

    const detailsButton = heading.querySelector(".djep-eventdetailsbutton");
    if (detailsButton) {
      detailsButton.textContent = "Event Details";
      detailsButton.classList.add("djep-plan-header-button");
    }

    Array.from(heading.childNodes).forEach((node) => {
      if (node !== detailsButton) {
        node.remove();
      }
    });

    const titleNode = document.createElement("span");
    titleNode.className = "djep-plan-title";
    titleNode.textContent = "Plan My Event";
    if (detailsButton) {
      heading.insertBefore(titleNode, detailsButton);
    } else {
      heading.append(titleNode);
    }

    const meta = document.createElement("div");
    meta.className = "djep-plan-meta";
    if (eventDateText) {
      meta.append(createMetaChip("Date", formatShortDate(eventDate) || eventDateText));
    }
    // The "Focus" chip was derived from the first planning form's name,
    // which is arbitrary and not always client-friendly. Dropped — the
    // Date chip plus the subtitle already give all the context needed.
    if (meta.children.length) {
      heading.append(meta);
    }

    const subtitle = document.createElement("div");
    subtitle.className = "djep-plan-subtitle";
    subtitle.textContent = longEventDate
      ? `Access music, forms, timeline, and print tools for ${longEventDate}.`
      : "Access music, forms, timeline, and print tools for this event.";
    heading.append(subtitle);
  }

  function setPlanPageSectionTitles(sectionMap) {
    const setTitlebarText = (box, text) => {
      const titlebar = box?.querySelector(":scope > .djep-titlebar");
      if (!titlebar) return;
      titlebar.textContent = text;
    };

    sectionMap.forEach(([box, text]) => setTitlebarText(box, text));
  }

  function enhancePlanList(box, noteText) {
    if (!box) return;

    box.querySelectorAll("table tr").forEach((row) => {
      const cells = row.querySelectorAll("td");
      if (cells.length < 3) return;

      const titleCell = cells[1];
      if (!titleCell.querySelector(".djep-plan-entry-copy")) {
        const titleText = cleanText(titleCell.textContent || "");
        titleCell.textContent = "";

        const copy = document.createElement("div");
        copy.className = "djep-plan-entry-copy";

        const title = document.createElement("div");
        title.className = "djep-plan-entry-title";
        title.textContent = titleText;

        copy.append(title);

        if (noteText) {
          const note = document.createElement("div");
          note.className = "djep-plan-entry-note";
          note.textContent = noteText;
          copy.append(note);
        }

        titleCell.append(copy);
      }

      const buttons = Array.from(cells[2].querySelectorAll(".djep-readviewbutton"));
      const editButton = buttons.find((button) => /edit/i.test(button.textContent || ""));
      if (editButton) {
        editButton.classList.add("djep-plan-primary-button");
      }

      // Strip whitespace text nodes between Edit/View buttons so the
      // mobile flex column doesn't render them as 0-height flex items
      // (which adds an unwanted gap between the stacked buttons).
      Array.from(cells[2].childNodes).forEach((node) => {
        if (node.nodeType === 3 && !(node.textContent || "").trim()) {
          node.remove();
        }
      });
    });
  }

  function normalizePlanningFormsHeading(pageHeading, {
    guardKey,
    headingClass,
    titleClass,
    titleText,
    subtitleClass,
    subtitleText,
    subtitleTag = "div",
  }) {
    if (!(pageHeading instanceof HTMLElement) || pageHeading.dataset[guardKey]) return;
    pageHeading.dataset[guardKey] = "1";
    pageHeading.classList.add(headingClass);

    const optionsButton = pageHeading.querySelector(".djep-planeventbutton");
    if (optionsButton && !optionsButton.dataset.djepLabelNormalized) {
      optionsButton.dataset.djepLabelNormalized = "1";
      optionsButton.textContent = "Planning Options";
    }

    Array.from(pageHeading.childNodes).forEach((node) => {
      if (node !== optionsButton) node.remove();
    });

    const title = document.createElement("span");
    title.className = titleClass;
    title.textContent = titleText;

    if (optionsButton) {
      pageHeading.insertBefore(title, optionsButton);
    } else {
      pageHeading.append(title);
    }

    const subtitle = document.createElement(subtitleTag);
    subtitle.className = subtitleClass;
    subtitle.textContent = subtitleText;
    pageHeading.append(subtitle);
  }

  function normalizePlanningFormsEditHeading(pageHeading, formTitle) {
    normalizePlanningFormsHeading(pageHeading, {
      guardKey: "djepPlanningFormHeadingInit",
      headingClass: "djep-planningform-heading",
      titleClass: "djep-planningform-title",
      titleText: "Planning Form",
      subtitleClass: "djep-planningform-subtitle",
      subtitleText: `Review and update the details for ${formTitle}.`,
    });
  }

  function normalizePlanningFormsViewHeading(pageHeading, formTitle) {
    normalizePlanningFormsHeading(pageHeading, {
      guardKey: "djepPlanningFormViewHeadingInit",
      headingClass: "djep-planningform-heading",
      titleClass: "djep-planningform-title",
      titleText: "Planning Form",
      subtitleClass: "djep-document-subtitle",
      subtitleText: `Review the saved answers for ${formTitle}.`,
      subtitleTag: "span",
    });
  }

  function normalizePlanningFormsLandingHeading(pageHeading) {
    normalizePlanningFormsHeading(pageHeading, {
      guardKey: "djepPlanningFormsLandingHeadingInit",
      headingClass: "djep-planningformslanding-heading",
      titleClass: "djep-planningformslanding-title",
      titleText: "Planning Forms",
      subtitleClass: "djep-planningformslanding-subtitle",
      subtitleText: "Choose the worksheet you want to edit or preview for this event.",
    });
  }

  function bindPaymentAmountValidation(form) {
    if (!(form instanceof HTMLElement) || form.dataset.djepAmountValidationBound === "1") return;
    form.dataset.djepAmountValidationBound = "1";

    form.addEventListener("submit", (event) => {
      const amountInput = form.querySelector("#amountdollars");
      const amountValue = (amountInput?.value || "").trim();
      if (!amountInput || amountValue) return;

      event.preventDefault();
      amountInput.setCustomValidity("Please enter a payment amount.");
      amountInput.reportValidity();
      amountInput.focus();
    });

    form.addEventListener("input", (event) => {
      if (event.target?.id !== "amountdollars") return;
      event.target.setCustomValidity("");
    });
  }

  function mountPaymentHeadingSubtitle({ root, form, heading, isAmountStep }) {
    if (!(heading instanceof HTMLElement)) return;

    heading.querySelectorAll(".djep-payment-subtitle").forEach((node) => node.remove());
    root?.querySelectorAll(":scope > .djep-payment-subtitle").forEach((node) => node.remove());
    form?.querySelectorAll(":scope > .djep-payment-subtitle").forEach((node) => node.remove());
    // Authorize.net (and any gateway where DJEP wraps the heading in its own
    // div) renders the subtitle as a sibling of the heading rather than a
    // direct child of root/form. Remove that too so we don't end up with
    // duplicates.
    let nextSib = heading.nextElementSibling;
    while (nextSib?.classList?.contains("djep-payment-subtitle")) {
      const toRemove = nextSib;
      nextSib = nextSib.nextElementSibling;
      toRemove.remove();
    }

    const subtitle = document.createElement("p");
    subtitle.className = "djep-payment-subtitle";
    subtitle.textContent = isAmountStep
      ? "Choose your payment method, enter the amount you want to pay, and continue securely to checkout."
      : "Review your payment options and billing details to complete checkout securely.";
    heading.insertAdjacentElement("afterend", subtitle);
  }

  function parsePaymentGatewayDetails(gatewayNotes) {
    if (!(gatewayNotes instanceof HTMLElement)) return null;

    const notesClone = gatewayNotes.cloneNode(true);
    notesClone
      .querySelectorAll("title, style, script, #submit_payment_button_row, .metro-button")
      .forEach((node) => node.remove());

    const links = Array.from(notesClone.querySelectorAll("a[href]")).map((link) => {
      const image = link.querySelector("img");
      return {
        href: link.getAttribute("href") || link.href || "",
        alt: image?.getAttribute("alt") || "",
        src: image?.getAttribute("src") || "",
      };
    });

    const text = cleanText(notesClone.textContent);
    const addressMatch = text.match(/Mailing Address:\s*(.+)$/i);
    const addressText = addressMatch ? cleanText(addressMatch[1]) : "";
    const introText = addressMatch ? cleanText(text.slice(0, addressMatch.index)) : text;
    // Look for a fee disclaimer in two places: a "Please note,..." sentence
    // (Stripe / generic) OR a `.djep-pay-fee-note` element (DJEP's own custom
    // class for fee text on gateway notes, used by some portals). Either way
    // the extracted text feeds the dynamic warning injection so each portal's
    // own admin-configured fee disclaimer shows up correctly.
    //
    // If the source text doesn't already start with a "Note" / "Please note"
    // prefix, add one — matches the pre-redesign visual where the disclaimer
    // always read as a "Note: ..." callout.
    const warningMatch = introText.match(/Please note,[^.]+\./i);
    const feeNoteEl = notesClone.querySelector(".djep-pay-fee-note");
    const feeNoteText = feeNoteEl ? cleanText(feeNoteEl.textContent || "") : "";
    let warningText = warningMatch
      ? cleanText(warningMatch[0])
      : feeNoteText || "";
    if (warningText && !/^(note|please note)\b/i.test(warningText)) {
      warningText = "Note: " + warningText;
    }
    const detailText = cleanText(introText.replace(warningText, ""));

    return {
      addressText,
      detailText,
      links,
      warningText,
    };
  }

  function derivePaymentGatewayDetailsFromAltBox(altBox) {
    if (!(altBox instanceof HTMLElement)) return null;

    const existingLinks = Array.from(altBox.querySelectorAll(".djep-payment-altlink[href]")).map((link) => {
      const image = link.querySelector("img");
      return {
        href: link.getAttribute("href") || link.href || "",
        alt: image?.getAttribute("alt") || cleanText(link.textContent || ""),
        src: image?.getAttribute("src") || "",
      };
    });
    const existingAddress = cleanText(
      (altBox.querySelector(".djep-payment-mailing")?.textContent || "").replace(/^Mailing Address:\s*/i, "")
    );

    return {
      addressText: existingAddress,
      detailText: "",
      links: existingLinks,
      warningText: "",
    };
  }

  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  // Conditional alt-payment buttons sourced from DJEP's gateway tabs
  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  // Goal: the "Other Ways to Pay" buttons (Venmo / Cash App / Zelle / etc.)
  // appear ONLY when the corresponding DJEP gateway tab is filled in. No
  // custom HTML required.
  //
  // How it works: we issue 3 same-origin fetches against the client portal's
  // own makeapayment.asp endpoint (no admin auth needed — the client is
  // already logged in for these requests). Each fetch returns a page that
  // either contains the configured handle/URL or doesn't.
  //   - ?action=venmo   → look for venmo.com/<handle>
  //   - ?action=cashapp → look for cash.app/$<handle>
  //   - no action       → look for the Custom tab's external URL
  // A gateway with no handle/URL detected is skipped (no button rendered).
  //
  // Branded images: see `getAltPaymentImageDefaults()` below. Each user can
  // override per-button via DJEP's "Custom Button Wording" fields where
  // they exist (see Custom tab). Images otherwise fall back to neutral
  // defaults shipped with the redesign.

  function getAltPaymentImageDefaults() {
    // Image URL resolution, in priority order:
    //   1. Per-portal override via window.DJEP_PAYMENT_BUTTON_IMAGES
    //   2. DJEP-bundled images at /images/paywith<gateway>.png — every DJEP
    //      install ships paywithvenmo.png and paywithcashapp.png at this path
    //      (verified — they're what DJEP's native Venmo/Cash App gateway pages
    //      load themselves). Zelle is NOT bundled by DJEP, so it falls
    //      through to the host-relative fallback.
    //   3. Host-relative fallback — resolves the image alongside the user's
    //      deployed djep-live.css file (so users hosting on GitHub Pages just
    //      drop the PNG into the same repo as the CSS).
    const cssHost = (() => {
      const link = document.querySelector('link[href*="djep-live"]');
      if (!link) return null;
      try {
        const u = new URL(link.href, location.href);
        u.pathname = u.pathname.replace(/\/[^\/]+$/, "/");
        return u.toString();
      } catch (e) { return null; }
    })();
    const cssRelative = cssHost ? (name) => cssHost + name : (name) => "";
    const djepNative = (name) => "/images/" + name;
    const override = window.DJEP_PAYMENT_BUTTON_IMAGES || {};
    return {
      // Venmo and Cash App — DJEP ships these by default, every user gets them for free
      venmo:   override.venmo   || djepNative("paywithvenmo.png"),
      cashapp: override.cashapp || djepNative("paywithcashapp.png"),
      // Zelle is not a DJEP-native gateway, so no bundled image. Falls back
      // to host-relative; if missing, the button is skipped (img validation
      // happens before render).
      zelle:   override.zelle   || cssRelative("paywithzelle.png"),
    };
  }

  function detectConfiguredAltGateways(eventid) {
    if (!eventid) return Promise.resolve({ venmo: null, cashapp: null, custom: null, customImage: null });
    const get = (action) =>
      fetch(`/clients/makeapayment.asp?eventid=${encodeURIComponent(eventid)}${action ? "&action=" + action : ""}`, { credentials: "include" })
        .then((r) => r.text())
        .catch(() => "");
    return Promise.all([get("venmo"), get("cashapp"), get("")]).then(([venmoHTML, cashappHTML, listHTML]) => {
      const venmoMatch = venmoHTML.match(/venmo\.com\/([A-Za-z0-9._-]+)/);
      const cashappMatch = cashappHTML.match(/cash\.app\/\$([A-Za-z0-9._-]+)/);

      let custom = null;
      let customImage = null;
      try {
        const doc = new DOMParser().parseFromString(listHTML, "text/html");
        for (const a of Array.from(doc.querySelectorAll("a[href]"))) {
          const href = a.getAttribute("href") || "";
          if (!/^https?:\/\//i.test(href)) continue;
          if (/venmo\.com|cash\.app|paypal|stripe|login\.abelldj|wp-content|\.png|\.jpg|\.gif/i.test(href)) continue;
          custom = href;
          // The link wrapping the Custom gateway button often contains an
          // <img> whose src is the custom_gateway_button_wording field
          // value from the Custom tab. Grab it as the user-configured
          // image for this Custom button (e.g., the Zelle PNG).
          const innerImg = a.querySelector("img[src]");
          if (innerImg) customImage = innerImg.getAttribute("src");
          break;
        }
        // Fallback: if no <img> nested in the link, look elsewhere on the
        // gateway-list page for any standalone image referenced near the
        // Custom URL (DJEP sometimes renders the button image in a sibling).
        if (custom && !customImage) {
          for (const img of Array.from(doc.querySelectorAll("img[src]"))) {
            const src = img.getAttribute("src") || "";
            // Skip DJEP's own bundled native gateway images and skip the
            // company logo / Stripe-powered-by image.
            if (/\/images\/paywith(venmo|cashapp)\.png$/i.test(src)) continue;
            if (/logo|powered_by_stripe|paywithdebitcredit/i.test(src)) continue;
            if (/\.(png|jpe?g|gif|webp|svg)(\?|$)/i.test(src)) {
              customImage = src;
              break;
            }
          }
        }
      } catch (e) { /* ignore parse errors */ }

      return {
        venmo: venmoMatch ? venmoMatch[1] : null,
        cashapp: cashappMatch ? cashappMatch[1] : null,
        custom,
        customImage,
      };
    });
  }

  function applyConfiguredAltPaymentButtons(form) {
    if (!(form instanceof HTMLElement) || form.dataset.djepAltGatewayApplied === "1") return;
    const eventid = new URLSearchParams(location.search).get("eventid");
    if (!eventid) return;
    form.dataset.djepAltGatewayApplied = "1";

    detectConfiguredAltGateways(eventid).then((config) => {
      const grid = form.querySelector(".djep-payment-altlinks");
      if (!grid) return;
      const images = getAltPaymentImageDefaults();
      const entries = [];
      if (config.venmo)
        entries.push({ kind: "venmo",   href: "https://venmo.com/" + config.venmo,   alt: "Pay with Venmo",    src: images.venmo });
      if (config.cashapp)
        entries.push({ kind: "cashapp", href: "https://cash.app/$" + config.cashapp, alt: "Pay with Cash App", src: images.cashapp });
      if (config.custom) {
        // Custom button image priority: the user's own Custom tab "Button
        // Wording / Image link" field (auto-detected from the gateway list
        // page) → otherwise our default fallback chain in
        // getAltPaymentImageDefaults() (host-relative or override).
        const customSrc = config.customImage
          ? new URL(config.customImage, location.href).toString()
          : images.zelle;
        entries.push({ kind: "zelle", href: config.custom, alt: "Pay with Zelle", src: customSrc });
      }

      const checkCard = grid.querySelector(".djep-payment-altcard--check");
      Array.from(grid.querySelectorAll(".djep-payment-altlink:not(.djep-payment-altcard--check)")).forEach((node) => node.remove());
      entries.forEach((item) => {
        if (!item.src) return; // skip if we couldn't resolve an image URL
        const a = document.createElement("a");
        a.className = "djep-payment-altlink";
        a.href = item.href;
        a.target = "_blank";
        a.rel = "noopener noreferrer";
        a.dataset.djepKind = item.kind;
        const img = document.createElement("img");
        img.className = "djep-payment-altimage";
        img.alt = item.alt;
        img.src = item.src;
        a.append(img);
        if (checkCard) grid.insertBefore(a, checkCard);
        else grid.append(a);
      });
    }).catch(() => { /* network errors: leave existing rendering intact */ });
  }

  function rebuildPaymentAmountEntryInner(inner) {
    if (!(inner instanceof HTMLElement) || inner.classList.contains("djep-payment-rebuilt")) return null;

    const balanceLabelCell = inner.querySelector("#text_balancedue")?.closest(".col-xs-6");
    const balanceValueCell = balanceLabelCell?.nextElementSibling;
    const amountLabelCell = inner.querySelector("#text_enteramount")?.closest(".col-xs-6");
    const amountValueCell = inner.querySelector("#payment_amount")?.closest(".col-xs-6");
    const submitLabelCell = inner.querySelector("#text_paynow")?.closest(".col-xs-6");
    const submitValueCell = submitLabelCell?.nextElementSibling;
    const amountInput = inner.querySelector("#amountdollars");
    const submitButton = inner.querySelector('button[type="submit"], .djep-actionbutton');
    const totalAfter = inner.querySelector("#total_after_charges");

    if (
      !balanceLabelCell ||
      !balanceValueCell ||
      !amountLabelCell ||
      !amountValueCell ||
      !submitLabelCell ||
      !submitValueCell ||
      !amountInput ||
      !submitButton
    ) {
      return null;
    }

    const balanceAmount = cleanText(balanceValueCell.textContent) || "$0.00";
    const currencySymbol = extractCurrencySymbol(balanceAmount) || "$";

    inner.querySelectorAll(':scope > .cf, :scope > div[style*="height"], :scope > .form-group').forEach((node) => node.remove());

    const summaryCard = document.createElement("section");
    summaryCard.className = "djep-payment-card djep-payment-summary-card";

    const summaryLabel = document.createElement("span");
    summaryLabel.className = "djep-payment-card-label";
    summaryLabel.textContent = "Current Balance Due";

    const summaryValue = document.createElement("div");
    summaryValue.className = "djep-payment-balance-value";
    summaryValue.textContent = balanceAmount;
    summaryCard.append(summaryLabel, summaryValue);

    const amountCard = document.createElement("section");
    amountCard.className = "djep-payment-card djep-payment-amount-card";

    const amountLabel = document.createElement("span");
    amountLabel.className = "djep-payment-card-label";
    amountLabel.textContent = "Enter a Payment Amount";

    const amountCopy = document.createElement("p");
    amountCopy.className = "djep-payment-card-copy";
    amountCopy.textContent =
      "Enter the amount you want to pay today. You can review the total before continuing.";

    const amountField = document.createElement("div");
    amountField.className = "djep-payment-amount-field";

    const currency = document.createElement("span");
    currency.className = "djep-payment-currency";
    currency.textContent = currencySymbol;

    amountInput.removeAttribute("size");
    amountInput.setAttribute("inputmode", "decimal");
    amountInput.setAttribute("placeholder", "0.00");

    amountField.append(currency, amountInput);
    amountCard.append(amountLabel, amountCopy, amountField);

    if (totalAfter) {
      const charges = document.createElement("div");
      charges.className = "djep-payment-total-after";
      charges.append(totalAfter);
      amountCard.append(charges);
    }

    const actionCard = document.createElement("section");
    actionCard.className = "djep-payment-card djep-payment-submit-card";

    // No hardcoded label/copy here — just the submit button. Each portal's
    // submit button already carries its own DJEP-rendered text (e.g.
    // "Submit Payment" / "Continue" / etc.).
    actionCard.append(submitButton);

    inner.innerHTML = "";
    inner.classList.add("djep-payment-rebuilt");
    inner.append(summaryCard, amountCard, actionCard);

    return { summaryCard, amountCard, actionCard };
  }

  function ensurePaymentWorkspace(form) {
    if (!(form instanceof HTMLElement)) {
      return { workspace: null, mainColumn: null, sideColumn: null };
    }

    let workspace = form.querySelector(".djep-payment-workspace");
    let mainColumn = workspace?.querySelector(".djep-payment-column-main");
    let sideColumn = workspace?.querySelector(".djep-payment-column-side");

    if (!workspace) {
      workspace = document.createElement("div");
      workspace.className = "djep-payment-workspace";
      mainColumn = document.createElement("div");
      mainColumn.className = "djep-payment-column djep-payment-column-main";
      sideColumn = document.createElement("div");
      sideColumn.className = "djep-payment-column djep-payment-column-side";
      workspace.append(mainColumn, sideColumn);
    }

    return { workspace, mainColumn, sideColumn };
  }

  function mountPaymentWorkspace(form, heading, workspace) {
    if (!(form instanceof HTMLElement) || !(workspace instanceof HTMLElement) || form.contains(workspace)) return;

    const anchor =
      heading?.nextElementSibling?.classList?.contains("djep-payment-subtitle") ? heading.nextElementSibling : heading;
    if (anchor && anchor.parentElement === form) {
      anchor.insertAdjacentElement("afterend", workspace);
    } else {
      form.insertBefore(workspace, form.firstChild);
    }
  }

  function cleanupPaymentContentRoot(content, root) {
    if (!(content instanceof HTMLElement) || !(root instanceof HTMLElement) || root.parentElement !== content) return;

    root.classList.remove("payment_page_div", "djep-payment_page_div");
    root.classList.add("djep-payment-root");

    const form = root.querySelector(":scope > form");
    const heading = root.querySelector(":scope > h2.djep-h2");
    const subtitle = root.querySelector(":scope > .djep-payment-subtitle");

    // Some gateways (Authorize.net in particular) render their submit
    // button row as a SIBLING of #page_paypal inside #djep-content rather
    // than inside the form. Capture it and pull it into the form so our
    // workspace layout can pick it up. Without this, replaceChildren below
    // would discard the only submit control on the page.
    const strayButtonRow = content.querySelector(":scope > #submit_payment_button_row");
    if (strayButtonRow instanceof HTMLElement && form instanceof HTMLElement) {
      form.append(strayButtonRow);
    }

    if (form instanceof HTMLElement) {
      root.querySelectorAll(':scope > input[type="hidden"]').forEach((input) => {
        form.append(input);
      });
    }

    const nextRootChildren = [];
    if (heading instanceof HTMLElement) nextRootChildren.push(heading);
    if (subtitle instanceof HTMLElement) nextRootChildren.push(subtitle);
    if (form instanceof HTMLElement) nextRootChildren.push(form);
    if (nextRootChildren.length) {
      root.replaceChildren(...nextRootChildren);
    }

    const footer = content.querySelector(":scope > #footer");
    const nextChildren = [root];
    if (footer instanceof HTMLElement) {
      nextChildren.push(footer);
    }
    content.replaceChildren(...nextChildren);
  }

  function initializePaymentBillingAddressSection({ form, billingBox, altAddress }) {
    if (!(form instanceof HTMLElement) || !(billingBox instanceof HTMLElement) || !(altAddress instanceof HTMLElement)) return;

    const zipInput = altAddress.querySelector('input[name="address_zip"]');

    const forceAltAddressWidths = () => {
      altAddress.querySelectorAll(".col-xs-12.col-sm-6").forEach((node) => {
        node.style.width = "100%";
        node.style.maxWidth = "none";
        node.style.float = "none";
        node.style.paddingLeft = "0";
        node.style.paddingRight = "0";
      });

      altAddress.querySelectorAll(".col-xs-12.col-sm-3, .col-xs-12.col-sm-9").forEach((node) => {
        node.style.width = "100%";
        node.style.maxWidth = "none";
        node.style.float = "none";
        node.style.paddingLeft = "0";
        node.style.paddingRight = "0";
      });

      altAddress.querySelectorAll(".address_padding").forEach((node) => {
        node.style.width = "100%";
        node.style.maxWidth = "none";
        node.style.padding = "0 0 8px";
        node.style.display = "block";
      });

      altAddress
        .querySelectorAll('input[name^="address_"], select[name="address_country"], textarea[name^="address_"]')
        .forEach((node) => {
          node.style.width = "100%";
          node.style.maxWidth = "none";
          node.style.display = "block";
          node.style.boxSizing = "border-box";
        });
    };

    const normalizeAltAddressLayout = () => {
      const needsNormalization =
        !altAddress.querySelector(".djep-payment-alt-address-fields") || Boolean(altAddress.querySelector(".address_padding"));

      if (!needsNormalization) return;

      const titlebar = altAddress.querySelector(":scope > .djep-titlebar");
      const labels = Array.from(altAddress.querySelectorAll(".address_padding"))
        .map((node) => cleanText(node.textContent || ""))
        .filter(Boolean);
      const controls = Array.from(altAddress.querySelectorAll("input, select, textarea")).filter(
        (node) => !["hidden", "radio", "checkbox"].includes((node.getAttribute("type") || "").toLowerCase())
      );

      if (labels.length && controls.length) {
        const rowsHost = document.createElement("div");
        rowsHost.className = "djep-payment-alt-address-fields";

        labels.forEach((labelText, index) => {
          const control = controls[index];
          if (!control) return;

          const row = document.createElement("div");
          row.className = "djep-payment-alt-row";

          const label = document.createElement("label");
          label.className = "djep-payment-alt-label";
          label.textContent = labelText;

          if (!control.id) {
            control.id = `djep-alt-address-${index + 1}`;
          }
          label.setAttribute("for", control.id);

          const controlWrap = document.createElement("div");
          controlWrap.className = "djep-payment-alt-control";
          control.classList.add("djep-payment-alt-input");
          controlWrap.append(control);

          row.append(label, controlWrap);
          rowsHost.append(row);
        });

        altAddress.querySelectorAll(":scope > :not(.djep-titlebar)").forEach((node) => node.remove());
        if (titlebar) {
          altAddress.append(rowsHost);
        } else {
          altAddress.prepend(rowsHost);
        }
        altAddress.dataset.djepNormalized = "1";
      }

      forceAltAddressWidths();
    };

    const defaultAddressRadio = billingBox.querySelector("#use_profile_address");
    const newAddressRadio = billingBox.querySelector("#use_new_address");

    const syncBillingAddressVisibility = () => {
      normalizeAltAddressLayout();
      forceAltAddressWidths();
      const shouldShow = Boolean(newAddressRadio?.checked) && !Boolean(defaultAddressRadio?.checked);
      altAddress.style.display = shouldShow ? "block" : "none";
      altAddress.hidden = !shouldShow;
      altAddress.setAttribute("aria-hidden", shouldShow ? "false" : "true");
      altAddress.classList.toggle("is-open", shouldShow);
      if (zipInput) {
        zipInput.required = shouldShow;
        if (!shouldShow) {
          zipInput.setCustomValidity("");
        }
      }
    };

    const validateBillingZipRequirement = () => {
      if (!zipInput || !newAddressRadio?.checked || Boolean(defaultAddressRadio?.checked)) {
        zipInput?.setCustomValidity("");
        return true;
      }
      const zipValue = String(zipInput.value || "").trim();
      if (zipValue) {
        zipInput.setCustomValidity("");
        return true;
      }
      zipInput.setCustomValidity("Please enter a billing ZIP code.");
      zipInput.reportValidity();
      zipInput.focus();
      return false;
    };

    billingBox.querySelectorAll('input[name="billing_address"]').forEach((input) => {
      if (input.dataset.djepBillingBound === "1") return;
      input.dataset.djepBillingBound = "1";
      input.addEventListener("change", syncBillingAddressVisibility);
      input.addEventListener("click", syncBillingAddressVisibility);
    });

    if (zipInput && zipInput.dataset.djepZipBound !== "1") {
      zipInput.dataset.djepZipBound = "1";
      zipInput.addEventListener("input", () => {
        zipInput.setCustomValidity("");
      });
      zipInput.addEventListener("change", () => {
        zipInput.setCustomValidity("");
      });
    }

    if (form.dataset.djepBillingZipValidationBound !== "1") {
      form.dataset.djepBillingZipValidationBound = "1";
      form.addEventListener(
        "submit",
        (event) => {
          if (validateBillingZipRequirement()) return;
          event.preventDefault();
        },
        true
      );
    }

    syncBillingAddressVisibility();
    window.setTimeout(syncBillingAddressVisibility, 0);
    window.setTimeout(syncBillingAddressVisibility, 120);
    window.setTimeout(syncBillingAddressVisibility, 400);
    window.setTimeout(syncBillingAddressVisibility, 900);

    const billingObserver = new MutationObserver(() => {
      forceAltAddressWidths();
      if (altAddress.querySelector(".address_padding")) {
        normalizeAltAddressLayout();
      }
    });
    billingObserver.observe(altAddress, { childList: true, subtree: true });
  }

  function bindPaymentSubmitRecovery({ form, submitRow, errorBox, mainCard, cardholderName }) {
    if (!(form instanceof HTMLElement)) return;

    const submitButton = submitRow?.querySelector('button[type="submit"], input[type="submit"]');
    const getSubmitButtonLabel = () => {
      if (!submitButton) return "";
      if (submitButton instanceof HTMLInputElement) {
        return submitButton.value || "";
      }
      return submitButton.textContent || "";
    };
    const setSubmitButtonLabel = (label) => {
      if (!submitButton) return;
      if (submitButton instanceof HTMLInputElement) {
        submitButton.value = label;
        return;
      }
      submitButton.textContent = label;
    };
    const rememberSubmitButtonLabel = () => {
      if (!submitButton) return;
      const currentLabel = cleanText(getSubmitButtonLabel());
      if (!currentLabel || /processing/i.test(currentLabel)) return;
      submitButton.dataset.djepOriginalLabel = currentLabel;
    };
    const getStoredSubmitButtonLabel = () =>
      submitButton?.dataset.djepOriginalLabel || submitButton?.getAttribute("data-originalvalue") || "Pay Now";
    const hasBlockingPaymentError = () => {
      const hasCardholderError = Boolean(cardholderName) && !String(cardholderName.value || "").trim();
      const errorText = cleanText(errorBox?.textContent || "");
      const hasStripeFieldError = Boolean(
        mainCard?.querySelector(".StripeElement--invalid, .StripeElement--empty.invalid, .invalid")
      );
      return hasCardholderError || Boolean(errorText) || hasStripeFieldError;
    };
    const restoreSubmitButtonIfBlocked = () => {
      if (!submitButton) return;
      const currentLabel = cleanText(getSubmitButtonLabel());
      if (!submitButton.disabled && !/processing/i.test(currentLabel)) return;
      if (!hasBlockingPaymentError()) return;
      submitButton.disabled = false;
      submitButton.removeAttribute("disabled");
      submitButton.removeAttribute("aria-busy");
      setSubmitButtonLabel(getStoredSubmitButtonLabel());
    };
    const scheduleSubmitButtonRecovery = () => {
      window.setTimeout(restoreSubmitButtonIfBlocked, 120);
      window.setTimeout(restoreSubmitButtonIfBlocked, 450);
      window.setTimeout(restoreSubmitButtonIfBlocked, 900);
    };

    rememberSubmitButtonLabel();
    if (submitButton && submitButton.dataset.djepRecoveryBound !== "1") {
      submitButton.dataset.djepRecoveryBound = "1";
      submitButton.addEventListener(
        "click",
        () => {
          rememberSubmitButtonLabel();
          scheduleSubmitButtonRecovery();
        },
        true
      );
    }
    if (form.dataset.djepSubmitRecoveryBound !== "1") {
      form.dataset.djepSubmitRecoveryBound = "1";
      form.addEventListener(
        "submit",
        () => {
          rememberSubmitButtonLabel();
          scheduleSubmitButtonRecovery();
        },
        true
      );
    }
    if (errorBox && errorBox.dataset.djepRecoveryObserved !== "1") {
      errorBox.dataset.djepRecoveryObserved = "1";
      const paymentErrorObserver = new MutationObserver(() => {
        restoreSubmitButtonIfBlocked();
      });
      paymentErrorObserver.observe(errorBox, {
        childList: true,
        subtree: true,
        characterData: true,
      });
    }
    mainCard?.querySelectorAll("input, select, textarea").forEach((field) => {
      if (!(field instanceof HTMLElement) || field.dataset.djepRecoveryBound === "1") return;
      field.dataset.djepRecoveryBound = "1";
      field.addEventListener("input", restoreSubmitButtonIfBlocked);
      field.addEventListener("change", restoreSubmitButtonIfBlocked);
    });
    cardholderName?.addEventListener("input", restoreSubmitButtonIfBlocked);
    restoreSubmitButtonIfBlocked();
  }

  function renderPaymentGatewayAltBox({ form, paymentBox, gatewayNotes, gatewayDetails }) {
    if (!(form instanceof HTMLElement) || !gatewayDetails) {
      return form?.querySelector(".djep-payment-altbox") || null;
    }

    let altBox = form.querySelector(".djep-payment-altbox");
    if (!altBox) {
      altBox = document.createElement("section");
      altBox.className = "djep-payment-altbox";
      form.insertBefore(altBox, paymentBox?.nextSibling || null);
    }

    altBox.innerHTML = "";

    const altTitle = document.createElement("p");
    altTitle.className = "djep-titlebarsmall";
    altTitle.textContent = "Other Ways to Pay";
    altBox.append(altTitle);

    const altContent = document.createElement("div");
    altContent.className = "djep-payment-altcontent";

    const linkGrid = document.createElement("div");
    linkGrid.className = "djep-payment-altlinks";

    gatewayDetails.links.forEach((item) => {
      const link = document.createElement("a");
      link.className = "djep-payment-altlink";
      link.href = normalizePaymentProviderHref(item.href || "");
      link.target = "_blank";
      link.rel = "noopener noreferrer";
      const image = document.createElement("img");
      image.className = "djep-payment-altimage";
      image.alt = item.alt;
      image.src = item.src;
      link.append(image);
      linkGrid.append(link);
    });

    const checkCard = document.createElement("div");
    checkCard.className = "djep-payment-altlink djep-payment-altcard djep-payment-altcard--check";

    const checkLabel = document.createElement("span");
    checkLabel.className = "djep-payment-altlink-label";
    checkLabel.textContent = "Pay by Check";

    const checkAddress = document.createElement("span");
    checkAddress.className = "djep-payment-altcheck-address";
    checkAddress.textContent =
      cleanText(gatewayDetails.addressText || "") || readCompanyMailingAddressSync() || "Mailing address unavailable.";

    checkCard.append(checkLabel, checkAddress);
    linkGrid.append(checkCard);

    void getCompanyMailingAddress(gatewayDetails.addressText || "").then((addressText) => {
      const resolvedAddress = cleanText(addressText || "");
      if (!resolvedAddress || !checkAddress.isConnected) return;
      checkAddress.textContent = resolvedAddress;
    });

    altContent.append(linkGrid);
    altBox.append(altContent);
    retargetExistingPaymentAltLinks(form);
    gatewayNotes?.remove();

    return altBox;
  }

  function buildPaymentAltCopyHtml() {
    return (
      '<span class="djep-payment-alt-copy-line"><strong>Include event date and name on account when submitting.</strong></span>' +
      '<span class="djep-payment-alt-copy-line">Do NOT mark as a "Good or Service".</span>' +
      '<span class="djep-payment-alt-copy-line">Payments are manually processed and you will receive a confirmation email when applied.</span>'
    );
  }

  function buildStripeDetailsPaymentStep({ root, form, heading }) {
    root.classList.add("djep-payment-stripe-root");

    const requestButton = form.querySelector("#payment-request-button");
    const mainCard = form.querySelector("#maincarddiv");
    const legacyCardTitle =
      mainCard?.previousElementSibling && mainCard.previousElementSibling.classList.contains("djep-titlebar")
        ? mainCard.previousElementSibling
        : null;
    const billingBox = form.querySelector("#djep-billingcheckbox");
    const altAddress = form.querySelector("#alternative_card_address");
    const submitRow = form.querySelector("#card-submit");
    const errorBox = form.querySelector("#card-errors");
    const cardholderName = form.querySelector('input[name="cardholder_name"]');

    requestButton?.classList.add("djep-payment-wallet-box");
    mainCard?.classList.add("djep-payment-card-entry");
    billingBox?.classList.add("djep-payment-billing-box");
    submitRow?.classList.add("djep-payment-submit-row");
    errorBox?.classList.add("djep-payment-error-box");

    const { workspace, mainColumn, sideColumn } = ensurePaymentWorkspace(form);

    const paymentPanel =
      workspace.querySelector(".djep-payment-panel.djep-payment-details-panel") || document.createElement("section");
    if (!paymentPanel.classList.contains("djep-payment-panel")) {
      paymentPanel.className = "djep-payment-panel djep-payment-details-panel";
    }

    if (!paymentPanel.querySelector(":scope > .djep-titlebarsmall")) {
      const panelTitle = document.createElement("p");
      panelTitle.className = "djep-titlebarsmall";
      panelTitle.textContent = "Payment Details";
      paymentPanel.append(panelTitle);
    }

    if (billingBox && cardholderName && !paymentPanel.querySelector(".djep-payment-cardholder-block")) {
      const labelCell = cardholderName.closest(".col-xs-12.col-sm-9")?.previousElementSibling;
      const inputCell = cardholderName.closest(".col-xs-12.col-sm-9");
      const cardholderBlock = document.createElement("div");
      cardholderBlock.className = "djep-payment-cardholder-block";

      const cardholderLabel = document.createElement("label");
      cardholderLabel.className = "djep-payment-cardholder-label";
      cardholderLabel.setAttribute("for", "djep-cardholder-name");
      cardholderLabel.textContent = cleanText(labelCell?.textContent || "Card Holder Name");

      cardholderName.id = "djep-cardholder-name";
      cardholderName.classList.add("djep-payment-cardholder-input");

      cardholderBlock.append(cardholderLabel, cardholderName);
      paymentPanel.append(cardholderBlock);

      labelCell?.remove();
      inputCell?.remove();

      billingBox.querySelectorAll(":scope > .cf, :scope > div[style*='height:5px']").forEach((node) => {
        if (node.previousElementSibling == null) node.remove();
      });
    }

    legacyCardTitle?.remove();
    if (mainCard) paymentPanel.append(mainCard);
    if (errorBox) paymentPanel.append(errorBox);
    if (submitRow) paymentPanel.append(submitRow);
    if (requestButton) {
      requestButton.querySelectorAll(":scope > .djep-titlebar").forEach((node) => node.remove());
      paymentPanel.append(requestButton);
    }
    mainColumn?.append(paymentPanel);

    if (billingBox) {
      let billingPanel =
        workspace.querySelector(".djep-payment-panel.djep-payment-billing-panel") || document.createElement("section");
      if (!billingPanel.classList.contains("djep-payment-panel")) {
        billingPanel.className = "djep-payment-panel djep-payment-billing-panel";
      }
      if (!billingPanel.querySelector(":scope > .djep-titlebarsmall")) {
        const panelTitle = document.createElement("p");
        panelTitle.className = "djep-titlebarsmall";
        panelTitle.textContent = "Billing Details";
        billingPanel.append(panelTitle);
      }
      billingBox.querySelectorAll(":scope > .djep-titlebar").forEach((node) => node.remove());
      billingPanel.append(billingBox);
      sideColumn?.append(billingPanel);
    }

    if (billingBox) {
      const customerEmailInput = billingBox.querySelector('input[name="customer_email"], input#customer_email');
      const customerEmailBlock = customerEmailInput?.closest(".form-group, .col-xs-12, .row, .djep-payment-email-block, div");
      if (customerEmailInput) {
        customerEmailInput.required = false;
        customerEmailInput.removeAttribute("required");
      }
      if (customerEmailBlock instanceof HTMLElement) {
        customerEmailBlock.style.display = "none";
        customerEmailBlock.setAttribute("aria-hidden", "true");
      }
    }

    if (billingBox && altAddress) {
      initializePaymentBillingAddressSection({ form, billingBox, altAddress });
    }

    const pruneWalletBox = () => {
      if (!requestButton) return;
      if (isLocalPreviewEnvironment()) {
        requestButton.style.display = "none";
        return;
      }
      const innerWallet = requestButton.querySelector("#inner-payment-request-button") || requestButton;
      const hasVisibleControl =
        !!innerWallet.querySelector("button, iframe, .payment-request-button, [role='button']") ||
        cleanText(innerWallet.textContent).length > 0;
      requestButton.style.display = hasVisibleControl ? "" : "none";
    };

    pruneWalletBox();
    window.setTimeout(pruneWalletBox, 450);
    window.setTimeout(pruneWalletBox, 1200);

    mountPaymentWorkspace(form, heading, workspace);

    if (cardholderName && !cardholderName.getAttribute("placeholder")) {
      cardholderName.setAttribute("placeholder", "Name on card");
    }

    bindPaymentSubmitRecovery({ form, submitRow, errorBox, mainCard, cardholderName });

    const duplicateWalletTitles = requestButton?.querySelectorAll(":scope > .djep-titlebar");
    if (duplicateWalletTitles && duplicateWalletTitles.length > 1) {
      duplicateWalletTitles.forEach((title, index) => {
        if (index > 0) title.remove();
      });
    }
  }

  function buildSquareDetailsPaymentStep({ root, form, heading, paymentBox }) {
    if (!(form instanceof HTMLElement) || !(paymentBox instanceof HTMLElement)) return;
    root.classList.add("djep-payment-square-root");

    // Step 1: Square renders `<form id="nonce-form">` INSIDE `.djep-makepaymentbox`,
    // which is the inverse of how DJEP renders Stripe (form is the outer
    // wrapper there). Lift the form out so it sits at root level — then we
    // can build the workspace inside it without creating a circular DOM op.
    const pbParent = paymentBox.parentElement;
    if (pbParent && paymentBox.contains(form)) {
      pbParent.insertBefore(form, paymentBox);
    }

    // Step 2: move heading + subtitle INTO the form so the structure mirrors
    // Stripe's amount-entry page exactly (#page_paypal > form > [h2, subtitle,
    // workspace]). The heading was at #page_paypal > div > h2 originally and
    // the subtitle (added by mountPaymentHeadingSubtitle) is wherever heading
    // sits.
    const subtitle = root.querySelector(":scope .djep-payment-subtitle");
    if (heading && heading.parentElement !== form) {
      form.insertBefore(heading, form.firstChild);
    }
    if (subtitle && heading) {
      heading.insertAdjacentElement("afterend", subtitle);
    }

    // Step 3: build the workspace inside the form.
    const { workspace, mainColumn, sideColumn } = ensurePaymentWorkspace(form);

    // Step 4: reuse the existing .djep-makepaymentbox as the main panel,
    // matching the Stripe-amount-entry visual exactly.
    paymentBox.classList.add("djep-payment-panel", "djep-payment-entry-panel");

    // Capture DJEP's server-rendered titlebar text BEFORE we strip it, so
    // the new titlebarsmall can preserve the portal's actual gateway wording
    // (e.g., "Pay with PayPal" / "Pay by Credit Card or Debit Card" / etc.)
    // instead of a hardcoded value.
    const originalSquareTitle = cleanText(
      paymentBox.querySelector(":scope > .djep-titlebar")?.textContent || ""
    );
    if (originalSquareTitle) {
      paymentBox.dataset.djepOriginalTitle = originalSquareTitle;
    }

    // Drop the original Square "Please enter the amount:" titlebar and the
    // separate "Please enter your card details" sub-title — both will be
    // replaced with our titlebarsmall + per-card labels.
    paymentBox
      .querySelectorAll(":scope > .djep-payment-titlebar, :scope > .djep-titlebar")
      .forEach((node) => node.remove());
    const cardDetailsTitle = Array.from(form.querySelectorAll(":scope > .djep-titlebar")).find((p) =>
      /card\s*details/i.test(p.textContent || "")
    );
    cardDetailsTitle?.remove();

    // Use DJEP's server-rendered titlebar text — preserves whatever each
    // portal's gateway calls itself (Stripe / Square / PayPal Pro / etc.).
    // Captured BEFORE we strip titlebars above, but if missing, fall back
    // to a neutral phrase rather than hardcoding a gateway name.
    const squareTitleSource =
      cleanText(paymentBox.dataset.djepOriginalTitle || "") ||
      "Make a Payment";
    let mainTitle = paymentBox.querySelector(":scope > .djep-titlebarsmall");
    if (!mainTitle) {
      mainTitle = document.createElement("p");
      mainTitle.className = "djep-titlebarsmall";
      paymentBox.prepend(mainTitle);
    }
    mainTitle.textContent = squareTitleSource;

    // Step 5: build the entry-grid with TWO cards side-by-side, matching
    // Stripe's 2-card layout (amount card + secondary card). For Square the
    // secondary card hosts the Square SDK card-container.
    let entryGrid = paymentBox.querySelector(":scope > .djep-payment-entry-grid");
    if (!entryGrid) {
      entryGrid = document.createElement("div");
      entryGrid.className = "djep-payment-entry-grid";
      mainTitle.insertAdjacentElement("afterend", entryGrid);
    }

    // Amount card built from Square's #maincarddiv_title. Square actually
    // has TWO inputs: #amount_nofee (visible, type="number") for the user to
    // type into, and #amount (type="hidden") that gets the synced value for
    // form submission. We move BOTH into the new amount card and only style
    // the visible one.
    const maincardWrap = form.querySelector("#maincarddiv_title");
    const amountInputVisible =
      form.querySelector("#amount_nofee") ||
      form.querySelector('input[type="number"][name="amount_nofee"]');
    const amountInputHidden = form.querySelector('#amount, input[name="amount"]');
    let balanceAmount = "$0.00";
    if (maincardWrap) {
      // Match any of the currencies extractCurrencySymbol recognises so the
      // balance shows in the portal's actual currency, not always dollars.
      const match = maincardWrap.textContent.match(/[\u00A3\u0024\u20AC\u00A5\u20B9\u20BD\u0E3F\u20A9\u20AA\u20BAR\u0024]\s?[\d,]+(?:\.\d{2})?/);
      if (match) balanceAmount = match[0].replace(/\s+/g, "");
    }
    const currencySymbol = extractCurrencySymbol(balanceAmount) || "$";

    if (amountInputVisible instanceof HTMLInputElement && maincardWrap && !maincardWrap.dataset.djepSquareRebuilt) {
      maincardWrap.dataset.djepSquareRebuilt = "1";
      const amountCard = document.createElement("section");
      amountCard.className = "djep-payment-card djep-payment-amount-card djep-payment-entry-maincard";

      const amountLabel = document.createElement("span");
      amountLabel.className = "djep-payment-card-label";
      amountLabel.textContent = "Enter a Payment Amount";

      const amountCopy = document.createElement("p");
      amountCopy.className = "djep-payment-card-copy";
      amountCopy.textContent =
        "Enter the amount you want to pay today.";

      const amountField = document.createElement("div");
      amountField.className = "djep-payment-amount-field";

      const currency = document.createElement("span");
      currency.className = "djep-payment-currency";
      currency.textContent = currencySymbol;

      amountInputVisible.removeAttribute("size");
      amountInputVisible.style.width = "";
      amountInputVisible.setAttribute("inputmode", "decimal");
      amountInputVisible.setAttribute("placeholder", "0.00");
      amountInputVisible.classList.add("djep-payment-amount-input");

      amountField.append(currency, amountInputVisible);
      amountCard.append(amountLabel, amountCopy, amountField);
      // Keep the hidden submission field inside the card so it submits with
      // the form regardless of cleanup that happens around the original wrap.
      if (amountInputHidden instanceof HTMLInputElement) {
        amountCard.append(amountInputHidden);
      }
      maincardWrap.replaceWith(amountCard);
      entryGrid.append(amountCard);
    }

    // Card details secondary card hosting #card-container.
    const cardContainer = form.querySelector("#card-container");
    if (cardContainer) {
      const cardCard = document.createElement("section");
      cardCard.className = "djep-payment-card djep-payment-card-entry-card djep-payment-entry-sidecard";
      const cardLabel = document.createElement("span");
      cardLabel.className = "djep-payment-card-label";
      cardLabel.textContent = "Card Details";
      const cardCopy = document.createElement("p");
      cardCopy.className = "djep-payment-card-copy";
      cardCopy.textContent = "Securely enter your card information.";
      cardContainer.classList.add("djep-payment-card-entry");
      cardCard.append(cardLabel, cardCopy, cardContainer);
      entryGrid.append(cardCard);
    }

    // Submit button below the entry grid.
    const submitBtn = form.querySelector("#submit_payment_button");
    if (submitBtn) {
      submitBtn.classList.add("djep-payment-submit-row");
      paymentBox.append(submitBtn);
    }

    // Step 6: side column — Current Balance Due + Billing Details panels.
    if (amountInputVisible) {
      const summaryPanel = document.createElement("section");
      summaryPanel.className = "djep-payment-panel djep-payment-summary-panel";
      const summaryTitle = document.createElement("p");
      summaryTitle.className = "djep-titlebarsmall";
      summaryTitle.textContent = "Current Balance Due";
      const summaryCard = document.createElement("section");
      summaryCard.className = "djep-payment-card djep-payment-summary-card";
      const summaryLabel = document.createElement("span");
      summaryLabel.className = "djep-payment-card-label";
      summaryLabel.textContent = "Current Balance Due";
      const summaryValue = document.createElement("div");
      summaryValue.className = "djep-payment-balance-value";
      summaryValue.textContent = balanceAmount;
      summaryCard.append(summaryLabel, summaryValue);
      summaryPanel.append(summaryTitle, summaryCard);
      sideColumn?.append(summaryPanel);
    }

    const billingBox = form.querySelector("#djep-billingcheckbox");
    if (billingBox) {
      billingBox.classList.add("djep-payment-billing-box");
      const billingPanel = document.createElement("section");
      billingPanel.className = "djep-payment-panel djep-payment-billing-panel";
      const billingTitle = document.createElement("p");
      billingTitle.className = "djep-titlebarsmall";
      billingTitle.textContent = "Billing Details";
      billingBox.querySelectorAll(":scope > .djep-titlebar").forEach((n) => n.remove());
      billingPanel.append(billingTitle, billingBox);
      sideColumn?.append(billingPanel);

      const altAddress = form.querySelector("#alternative_card_address");
      if (altAddress) {
        // Square's altAddress carries its own DJEP-rendered subheader
        // (a `.djep-titlebar > #text_paypalsubheader` that on some
        // portals reads "Pay with PayPal" because the gateway template
        // is shared with the legacy PayPal page). Drop it before any
        // layout normalization so the panel header is just our clean
        // "Billing Details" titlebarsmall.
        altAddress.querySelectorAll(":scope > .djep-titlebar").forEach((n) => n.remove());
        // Square's fields are named `cc_details_*` instead of
        // `address_*` — rebuild as labeled rows BEFORE
        // initializePaymentBillingAddressSection runs (its
        // normalizeAltAddressLayout only handles `address_*` controls
        // and would skip Square otherwise, leaving an unusable form).
        rebuildSquareAltAddressFields(altAddress);
        initializePaymentBillingAddressSection({ form, billingBox, altAddress });
      }
    }

    // Step 7: place paymentBox into the main column.
    mainColumn?.append(paymentBox);

    // Step 8: Mount the workspace into the form (after heading+subtitle).
    mountPaymentWorkspace(form, heading, workspace);

    // Step 9: alt-gateway buttons (Venmo / Cash App / Zelle), if configured.
    applyConfiguredAltPaymentButtons(form);
  }

  function rebuildSquareAltAddressFields(altAddress) {
    if (!(altAddress instanceof HTMLElement)) return;
    if (altAddress.dataset.djepSquareAltRebuilt === "1") return;

    // Collect the cc_details_* inputs/selects in DOM order so the row
    // ordering matches DJEP's "Address Line 1 / 2 / City / State / Zipcode".
    const controls = Array.from(
      altAddress.querySelectorAll(
        'input[name^="cc_details_"], select[name^="cc_details_"], textarea[name^="cc_details_"]'
      )
    ).filter((node) => !["hidden", "radio", "checkbox"].includes((node.getAttribute("type") || "").toLowerCase()));

    if (!controls.length) return;

    // Collect the matching DJEP-rendered labels from `.address_padding`
    // wrappers (DJEP uses the same wrapper class for cc_details fields).
    const labelNodes = Array.from(altAddress.querySelectorAll(".address_padding"));
    const labels = labelNodes.map((node) => cleanText(node.textContent || "")).filter(Boolean);

    const rowsHost = document.createElement("div");
    rowsHost.className = "djep-payment-alt-address-fields";

    controls.forEach((control, index) => {
      const labelText = labels[index] || control.name.replace(/^cc_details_/, "").replace(/_/g, " ");

      const row = document.createElement("div");
      row.className = "djep-payment-alt-row";

      const label = document.createElement("label");
      label.className = "djep-payment-alt-label";
      label.textContent = labelText;

      if (!control.id) {
        control.id = `djep-square-alt-${index + 1}`;
      }
      label.setAttribute("for", control.id);

      const controlWrap = document.createElement("div");
      controlWrap.className = "djep-payment-alt-control";
      control.classList.add("djep-payment-alt-input");
      control.style.width = "100%";
      control.style.maxWidth = "none";
      control.style.display = "block";
      control.style.boxSizing = "border-box";
      controlWrap.append(control);

      row.append(label, controlWrap);
      rowsHost.append(row);
    });

    // Remove ALL original children of altAddress (titlebar already gone)
    // — leaves a clean container we can prepend our labeled rows into.
    Array.from(altAddress.children).forEach((node) => {
      if (!node.contains(rowsHost)) node.remove();
    });
    altAddress.append(rowsHost);
    altAddress.dataset.djepSquareAltRebuilt = "1";
    altAddress.dataset.djepNormalized = "1";
  }

  function buildPaypalAmountEntryStep({ root, paymentBox }) {
    // PayPal renders WITHOUT a <form> wrapper. The Pay Now button
    // (#show_paypal_buttons) has an inline onclick that posts to PayPal.
    // We use #page_paypal itself as the workspace anchor, then rebuild
    // the visible UI into our Stripe-style two-column layout.
    if (!(root instanceof HTMLElement)) return;
    root.classList.add("djep-payment-root", "djep-payment-paypal-root");
    root.classList.remove("payment_page_div");

    // PayPal page has no server-rendered <h2.djep-h2> at root. Synthesize
    // a heading + subtitle so the page gets the same MAKE A PAYMENT title,
    // subtitle copy, and gradient hash divider that Stripe shows.
    let pageHeading = root.querySelector(":scope > h2.djep-h2");
    if (!pageHeading) {
      pageHeading = document.createElement("h2");
      pageHeading.className = "djep-h2";
      const headingSpan = document.createElement("span");
      headingSpan.id = "text_paypalpageheader";
      headingSpan.textContent = "Make A Payment";
      pageHeading.append(headingSpan);
      root.insertBefore(pageHeading, root.firstChild);
    }
    let pageSubtitle = root.querySelector(":scope > .djep-payment-subtitle");
    if (!pageSubtitle) {
      pageSubtitle = document.createElement("p");
      pageSubtitle.className = "djep-payment-subtitle";
      pageSubtitle.textContent =
        "Choose your payment method, enter the amount you want to pay, and continue securely to checkout.";
      pageHeading.insertAdjacentElement("afterend", pageSubtitle);
    }

    // Pull key elements out of DJEP's div-only markup.
    const mainForm = root.querySelector("#main-form");
    const titlebar = root.querySelector(":scope > .djep-titlebar");
    const balanceLabel = root.querySelector("#text_balancedue");
    const amountInput = root.querySelector("#paypal_amount");
    const submitButtonRow = root.querySelector("#submit_payment_button_row");
    const submitButton = root.querySelector("#show_paypal_buttons");
    const gatewayNotes = root.querySelector("#djep-gatewaychargenotes");
    const backLink = root.querySelector("a.djep-readviewbutton");
    const totalAfter = root.querySelector("#total_after_charges");

    // Balance from the cell that follows #text_balancedue. Match any
    // currency symbol so non-US portals (£ / € / etc.) show the right
    // value here and in the amount input below.
    let balanceAmount = "$0.00";
    if (balanceLabel) {
      const balanceCell = balanceLabel.closest("[class*='col-']");
      const valueCell = balanceCell?.nextElementSibling;
      const match = (valueCell?.textContent || "").match(/[\u00A3\u0024\u20AC\u00A5\u20B9\u20BD\u0E3F\u20A9\u20AA\u20BAR\u0024]\s?[\d,]+(?:\.\d{2})?/);
      if (match) balanceAmount = match[0].replace(/\s+/g, "");
    }
    const currencySymbol = extractCurrencySymbol(balanceAmount) || "$";

    // Capture DJEP's titlebar text BEFORE we strip it.
    const originalTitle = cleanText(titlebar?.textContent || "") || "Make a Payment";

    // Parse fee/warning note from gateway notes.
    const gatewayDetails = parsePaymentGatewayDetails(gatewayNotes);

    // Build workspace inside root (root acts as form anchor here).
    const { workspace, mainColumn, sideColumn } = ensurePaymentWorkspace(root);

    // Reuse or create the main panel.
    let panel = paymentBox;
    if (!(panel instanceof HTMLElement)) {
      panel = document.createElement("section");
    }
    panel.className = "djep-makepaymentbox djep-payment-panel djep-payment-entry-panel";
    // Clear panel — we'll rebuild from captured pieces.
    panel.replaceChildren();

    const mainTitle = document.createElement("p");
    mainTitle.className = "djep-titlebarsmall";
    mainTitle.textContent = originalTitle;
    panel.append(mainTitle);

    if (gatewayDetails?.warningText) {
      let warningText = gatewayDetails.warningText;
      if (!/^(note|please note)\b/i.test(warningText)) warningText = "Note: " + warningText;
      const warning = document.createElement("p");
      warning.className = "djep-payment-warning djep-payment-warning-inline";
      warning.textContent = warningText;
      panel.append(warning);
    }

    // Amount card.
    if (amountInput instanceof HTMLInputElement) {
      const amountCard = document.createElement("section");
      amountCard.className = "djep-payment-card djep-payment-amount-card djep-payment-entry-maincard";

      const amountLabel = document.createElement("span");
      amountLabel.className = "djep-payment-card-label";
      amountLabel.textContent = "Enter a Payment Amount";

      const amountCopy = document.createElement("p");
      amountCopy.className = "djep-payment-card-copy";
      amountCopy.textContent = "Enter the amount you want to pay today.";

      const amountField = document.createElement("div");
      amountField.className = "djep-payment-amount-field";

      const currency = document.createElement("span");
      currency.className = "djep-payment-currency";
      currency.textContent = currencySymbol;

      amountInput.removeAttribute("size");
      amountInput.style.width = "";
      amountInput.setAttribute("inputmode", "decimal");
      amountInput.setAttribute("placeholder", "0.00");
      amountInput.classList.add("djep-payment-amount-input");

      amountField.append(currency, amountInput);
      amountCard.append(amountLabel, amountCopy, amountField);

      // "Total After Charges:" — pull the whole .form-group (label + the
      // live-updated #total_after_charges value) into the card so the user
      // sees their running total below the input. Matches Stripe/Authnet.
      const totalAfterGroup = totalAfter?.closest(".form-group") || totalAfter;
      if (totalAfterGroup instanceof HTMLElement) {
        const charges = document.createElement("div");
        charges.className = "djep-payment-total-after";
        charges.append(totalAfterGroup);
        amountCard.append(charges);
      }

      panel.append(amountCard);
    }

    // Submit row (preserve inline onclick for PayPal redirect).
    if (submitButtonRow instanceof HTMLElement) {
      submitButtonRow.classList.add("djep-payment-submit-row");
      submitButtonRow.style.setProperty("margin-top", "18px", "important");
      panel.append(submitButtonRow);
    } else if (submitButton instanceof HTMLElement) {
      submitButton.classList.add("djep-payment-submit-row");
      submitButton.style.setProperty("margin-top", "18px", "important");
      panel.append(submitButton);
    }

    // Side column: Current Balance Due summary card.
    const summaryPanel = document.createElement("section");
    summaryPanel.className = "djep-payment-panel djep-payment-summary-panel";
    const summaryTitle = document.createElement("p");
    summaryTitle.className = "djep-titlebarsmall";
    summaryTitle.textContent = "Current Balance Due";
    const summaryCard = document.createElement("section");
    summaryCard.className = "djep-payment-card djep-payment-summary-card";
    const summaryLabel = document.createElement("span");
    summaryLabel.className = "djep-payment-card-label";
    summaryLabel.textContent = "Current Balance Due";
    const summaryValue = document.createElement("div");
    summaryValue.className = "djep-payment-balance-value";
    summaryValue.textContent = balanceAmount;
    summaryCard.append(summaryLabel, summaryValue);
    summaryPanel.append(summaryTitle, summaryCard);
    sideColumn?.append(summaryPanel);

    mainColumn?.append(panel);

    // Discard the now-empty original markup (titlebar, #main-form) so the
    // workspace is the only visible content under root.
    titlebar?.remove();
    if (mainForm && !workspace.contains(mainForm)) mainForm.remove();

    // Mount the workspace right after the synthesized heading+subtitle so
    // the page reads heading → subtitle (with its ::after gradient line) →
    // workspace, identical to Stripe's order.
    pageSubtitle.insertAdjacentElement("afterend", workspace);

    // Drop DJEP's full-width "Back" pill — the Stripe amount-entry step has
    // no such control, and matching it means losing this one. The browser
    // back button and the portal navigation both still get the user out.
    backLink?.remove();
  }

  function buildAuthorizenetEntryStep({ root, form, heading, paymentBox }) {
    if (!(form instanceof HTMLElement) || !(paymentBox instanceof HTMLElement)) return;
    root.classList.add("djep-payment-root", "djep-payment-authnet-root");
    root.classList.remove("payment_page_div");

    // Authorize.net's flow renders supporting elements (#submit_payment_button_row,
    // #card_details_iframe, #error_message_div, #backbuttonstate, inline scripts)
    // as SIBLINGS of #page_paypal inside #djep-content. We DON'T call
    // cleanupPaymentContentRoot for Authorize.net because it would discard them.
    // Instead, capture the ones we need to relocate ourselves.
    const content = document.getElementById("djep-content");
    const submitRow =
      content?.querySelector(":scope > #submit_payment_button_row") ||
      form.querySelector("#submit_payment_button_row");
    const cardDetailsIframe = content?.querySelector(":scope > #card_details_iframe");
    const errorMessageDiv = content?.querySelector(":scope > #error_message_div");
    const backButtonState = content?.querySelector(":scope > #backbuttonstate");

    // Title source: prefer the H2 page header (#text_paypalpageheader →
    // "Make A Payment"). The paymentBox titlebar on Authorize.net reads
    // "Enter your cards billing address" which is a section label, not the
    // page title.
    const originalTitle =
      cleanText(
        document.getElementById("text_paypalpageheader")?.textContent ||
          root.querySelector("h2.djep-h2")?.textContent ||
          ""
      ) || "Make a Payment";

    // Build the workspace inside the form.
    const { workspace, mainColumn, sideColumn } = ensurePaymentWorkspace(form);

    // Reshape paymentBox into the billing panel. Strip the original
    // DJEP titlebar FIRST, then call rebuildSquareAltAddressFields
    // (which removes all children except its rowsHost), then prepend our
    // titlebarsmall.
    paymentBox.querySelectorAll(":scope > .djep-titlebar").forEach((n) => n.remove());
    rebuildSquareAltAddressFields(paymentBox);

    paymentBox.classList.add("djep-payment-panel", "djep-payment-billing-panel");
    const billingTitle = document.createElement("p");
    billingTitle.className = "djep-titlebarsmall";
    billingTitle.textContent = "Billing Details";
    paymentBox.prepend(billingTitle);

    // Build the amount entry panel (main column).
    const amountPanel = document.createElement("section");
    amountPanel.className = "djep-makepaymentbox djep-payment-panel djep-payment-entry-panel";

    const mainTitle = document.createElement("p");
    mainTitle.className = "djep-titlebarsmall";
    mainTitle.textContent = originalTitle;
    amountPanel.append(mainTitle);

    const gatewayNotes = form.querySelector("#djep-gatewaychargenotes");
    const gatewayDetails = parsePaymentGatewayDetails(gatewayNotes);
    if (gatewayDetails?.warningText) {
      let warningText = gatewayDetails.warningText;
      if (!/^(note|please note)\b/i.test(warningText)) warningText = "Note: " + warningText;
      const warning = document.createElement("p");
      warning.className = "djep-payment-warning djep-payment-warning-inline";
      warning.textContent = warningText;
      amountPanel.append(warning);
    }

    // Amount card — Authorize.net uses Square-style #amount_nofee (visible)
    // + #amount (hidden, gets the synced value for submission).
    const amountInputVisible = form.querySelector("#amount_nofee");
    const amountInputHidden = form.querySelector('#amount, input[name="amount"]');
    const balanceValueCell = form
      .querySelector("#text_balancedue")
      ?.closest("[class*='col-']")?.nextElementSibling;
    // Match any currency symbol the portal might be configured with, not
    // just dollars — UK/EU portals would otherwise see "$" in the amount
    // input even though the balance is in £ / € / etc.
    let balanceAmount = "$0.00";
    const balMatch = (balanceValueCell?.textContent || "").match(/[\u00A3\u0024\u20AC\u00A5\u20B9\u20BD\u0E3F\u20A9\u20AA\u20BAR\u0024]\s?[\d,]+(?:\.\d{2})?/);
    if (balMatch) balanceAmount = balMatch[0].replace(/\s+/g, "");
    const currencySymbol = extractCurrencySymbol(balanceAmount) || "$";

    if (amountInputVisible instanceof HTMLInputElement) {
      const amountCard = document.createElement("section");
      amountCard.className = "djep-payment-card djep-payment-amount-card djep-payment-entry-maincard";
      const amountLabel = document.createElement("span");
      amountLabel.className = "djep-payment-card-label";
      amountLabel.textContent = "Enter a Payment Amount";
      const amountCopy = document.createElement("p");
      amountCopy.className = "djep-payment-card-copy";
      amountCopy.textContent = "Enter the amount you want to pay today.";
      const amountField = document.createElement("div");
      amountField.className = "djep-payment-amount-field";
      const currency = document.createElement("span");
      currency.className = "djep-payment-currency";
      currency.textContent = currencySymbol;
      amountInputVisible.removeAttribute("size");
      amountInputVisible.style.width = "";
      amountInputVisible.setAttribute("inputmode", "decimal");
      amountInputVisible.setAttribute("placeholder", "0.00");
      amountInputVisible.classList.add("djep-payment-amount-input");
      amountField.append(currency, amountInputVisible);
      amountCard.append(amountLabel, amountCopy, amountField);
      if (amountInputHidden instanceof HTMLInputElement) amountCard.append(amountInputHidden);

      // "Total After Charges:" — DJEP renders this as a .form-group
      // containing the label + the live-updated #total_after_charges value
      // span. Pull the whole form-group into the amount card so the user
      // sees their running total below the input, identical to Stripe.
      const totalAfterEl = form.querySelector("#total_after_charges");
      const totalAfterGroup = totalAfterEl?.closest(".form-group") || totalAfterEl;
      if (totalAfterGroup instanceof HTMLElement) {
        const charges = document.createElement("div");
        charges.className = "djep-payment-total-after";
        charges.append(totalAfterGroup);
        amountCard.append(charges);
      }

      amountPanel.append(amountCard);
    }

    if (submitRow instanceof HTMLElement) {
      submitRow.classList.add("djep-payment-submit-row");
      // A generic `p { margin: 0 !important }` reset in our CSS wins over
      // a plain inline margin-top. Use setProperty with 'important' so the
      // submit row gets visible breathing room beneath the amount input.
      submitRow.style.setProperty("margin-top", "18px", "important");
      amountPanel.append(submitRow);
    }

    mainColumn?.append(amountPanel);

    // Side column: Current Balance Due + Billing Details panels.
    const summaryPanel = document.createElement("section");
    summaryPanel.className = "djep-payment-panel djep-payment-summary-panel";
    const summaryTitle = document.createElement("p");
    summaryTitle.className = "djep-titlebarsmall";
    summaryTitle.textContent = "Current Balance Due";
    const summaryCard = document.createElement("section");
    summaryCard.className = "djep-payment-card djep-payment-summary-card";
    const summaryLabel = document.createElement("span");
    summaryLabel.className = "djep-payment-card-label";
    summaryLabel.textContent = "Current Balance Due";
    const summaryValue = document.createElement("div");
    summaryValue.className = "djep-payment-balance-value";
    summaryValue.textContent = balanceAmount;
    summaryCard.append(summaryLabel, summaryValue);
    summaryPanel.append(summaryTitle, summaryCard);
    sideColumn?.append(summaryPanel);

    sideColumn?.append(paymentBox);

    // Relocate the Accept.js card-details iframe holder, the error message
    // div, and the back-button state input into the form so they stay alive
    // and reachable by Authorize.net's openCreditCardWindowAuthorizeNetAcceptJS
    // handler. They're invisible UI helpers — no styling needed.
    if (cardDetailsIframe instanceof HTMLElement) {
      cardDetailsIframe.style.display = "none";
      form.append(cardDetailsIframe);
    }
    if (errorMessageDiv instanceof HTMLElement) {
      form.append(errorMessageDiv);
    }
    if (backButtonState instanceof HTMLInputElement) {
      form.append(backButtonState);
    }

    // Unwrap the heading + subtitle from DJEP's server-rendered wrapping
    // DIV so they become DIRECT children of the form, identical to the
    // Stripe layout (form > H2 > P.djep-payment-subtitle > .workspace).
    // This also lets mountPaymentWorkspace correctly place the workspace
    // after the subtitle (its anchor check requires anchor.parentElement
    // === form, which only succeeds with H2/subtitle at form-level).
    const headingWrapper = heading?.parentElement;
    if (
      headingWrapper instanceof HTMLElement &&
      headingWrapper !== form &&
      headingWrapper.parentElement === form &&
      headingWrapper.tagName === "DIV"
    ) {
      const subtitleEl = form.querySelector(":scope .djep-payment-subtitle");
      headingWrapper.insertAdjacentElement("beforebegin", heading);
      if (subtitleEl instanceof HTMLElement) {
        heading.insertAdjacentElement("afterend", subtitleEl);
      }
      headingWrapper.remove();
    }

    mountPaymentWorkspace(form, heading, workspace);

    // Hide remaining server-rendered shells that aren't part of our
    // workspace (the now-empty #user_info_div whose paymentBox we moved
    // out, and any stray "Please enter the amount" titlebar / balance
    // section sitting at form level). Kept in DOM (not removed) so any
    // inline scripts that reference these IDs still find them.
    const userInfoDiv = form.querySelector(":scope > #user_info_div");
    if (userInfoDiv instanceof HTMLElement) userInfoDiv.style.display = "none";
    Array.from(form.children).forEach((node) => {
      if (!(node instanceof HTMLElement)) return;
      if (node === workspace || node === heading) return;
      if (node.classList?.contains("djep-payment-subtitle")) return;
      if (node.id === "card_details_iframe" || node.id === "error_message_div" || node.id === "backbuttonstate") return;
      if (node.tagName === "INPUT" || node.tagName === "SCRIPT" || node.tagName === "STYLE") return;
      if (node.id === "user_info_div") return;
      if (node.querySelector(".djep-titlebar, .djep-titlebarsmall, #text_balancedue, #text_enteramount")) {
        node.style.display = "none";
      }
